OBX|1|TX|||Test~~Emergency Room~~The patient is a 39-year-old female who fell off a horse yesterday and~fractured her left clavicle.  She was referred down to see Dr. Smith today~because the physician who initially evaluated her felt that she would~likely require surgery for her clavicle fracture.  The patient does bring~along her films and in reviewing them it is very doubtful the patient will~require surgery.  I did share the films with Dr. Smith and he is in~agreement that at least at this point the patient will not require any type~of open procedure.  Will, therefore, continue to treat the patient with a~figure-of-8 splint and a sling.  She is requesting some stronger analgesics~as she was just placed on Darvocet, and this seems reasonable, so I did~prescribe some Vicodin for her.  Arrangements were made for a follow-up~appointment with Dr. Smith in the orthopedics clinic in approximately nine~days.  The patient works as an iron worker and certainly will not be able~to work at least immediately with her fractured clavicle, so she was~provided with a work excuse until she can follow up with Dr. Smith and he~can determine at which point she may be able to get back to work.

OBX|1|TX|||Test~~Emergency Room~~The patient is a 39-year-old female who fell off a horse yesterday and~fractured her left clavicle.  She was referred down to see Dr. Smith today~because the physician who initially evaluated her felt that she would~likely require surgery for her clavicle fracture.  The patient does bring~along her films and in reviewing them it is very doubtful the patient will~require surgery.  I did share the films with Dr. Smith and he is in~agreement that at least at this point the patient will not require any type~of open procedure.  Will, therefore, continue to treat the patient with a~figure-of-8 splint and a sling.  She is requesting some stronger analgesics~as she was just placed on Darvocet, and this seems reasonable, so I did~prescribe some Vicodin for her.  Arrangements were made for a follow-up~appointment with Dr. Smith in the orthopedics clinic in approximately nine~days.  The patient works as an iron worker and certainly will not be able~to work at least immediately with her fractured clavicle, so she was~provided with a work excuse until she can follow up with Dr. Smith and he~can determine at which point she may be able to get back to work.

OBX|1|TX|||Test~~Emergency Room~~The patient is a 39-year-old female who fell off a horse yesterday and~fractured her left clavicle.  She was referred down to see Dr. Smith today~because the physician who initially evaluated her felt that she would~likely require surgery for her clavicle fracture.  The patient does bring~along her films and in reviewing them it is very doubtful the patient will~require surgery.  I did share the films with Dr. Smith and he is in~agreement that at least at this point the patient will not require any type~of open procedure.  Will, therefore, continue to treat the patient with a~figure-of-8 splint and a sling.  She is requesting some stronger analgesics~as she was just placed on Darvocet, and this seems reasonable, so I did~prescribe some Vicodin for her.  Arrangements were made for a follow-up~appointment with Dr. Smith in the orthopedics clinic in approximately nine~days.  The patient works as an iron worker and certainly will not be able~to work at least immediately with her fractured clavicle, so she was~provided with a work excuse until she can follow up with Dr. Smith and he~can determine at which point she may be able to get back to work.

She was referred down to see Dr. Smith today~because the physician who initially evaluated her felt that she would~likely require surgery for her clavicle fracture.  The patient does bring~along her films and in reviewing them it is very doubtful the patient will~require surgery.  I did share the films with Dr. Smith and he is in~agreement that at least at this point the patient will not require any type~of open procedure.  Will, therefore, continue to treat the patient with a~figure-of-8 splint and a sling.  She is requesting some stronger analgesics~as she was just placed on Darvocet, and this seems reasonable, so I did~prescribe some Vicodin for her.  Arrangements were made for a follow-up~appointment with Dr. Smith in the orthopedics clinic in approximately nine~days.  The patient works as an iron worker and certainly will not be able~to work at least immediately with her fractured clavicle, so she was~provided with a work excuse until she can follow up with Dr. Smith and he~can determine at which point she may be able to get back to work.

She was referred down to see Dr. Smith today~because the physician who initially evaluated her felt that she would~likely require surgery for her clavicle fracture.  The patient does bring~along her films and in reviewing them it is very doubtful the patient will~require surgery. The patient works as an iron worker and certainly will not be able~to work at least immediately with her fractured clavicle, so she was~provided with a work excuse until she can follow up with Dr. Smith and he~can determine at which point she may be able to get back to work.

OBX|1|TX|||Test~~Emergency Room~~The patient is a 39-year-old female who fell off a horse yesterday and~fractured her left clavicle.  She was referred down to see Dr. Smith today~because the physician who initially evaluated her felt that she would~likely require surgery for her clavicle fracture.  The patient does bring~along her films and in reviewing them it is very doubtful the patient will~require surgery.  I did share the films with Dr. Smith and he is in~agreement that at least at this point the patient will not require any type~of open procedure.  Will, therefore, continue to treat the patient with a~figure-of-8 splint and a sling.  She is requesting some stronger analgesics~as she was just placed on Darvocet, and this seems reasonable, so I did~prescribe some Vicodin for her.  Arrangements were made for a follow-up~appointment with Dr. Smith in the orthopedics clinic in approximately nine~days.  The patient works as an iron worker and certainly will not be able~to work at least immediately with her fractured clavicle, so she was~provided with a work excuse until she can follow up with Dr. Smith and he~can determine at which point she may be able to get back to work.

OBX|1|TX|||Test~~Emergency Room~~The patient is a 39-year-old female who fell off a horse yesterday and~fractured her left clavicle.  She was referred down to see Dr. Smith today~because the physician who initially evaluated her felt that she would~likely require surgery for her clavicle fracture.  The patient does bring~along her films and in reviewing them it is very doubtful the patient will~require surgery.  I did share the films with Dr. Smith and he is in~agreement that at least at this point the patient will not require any type~of open procedure.  Will, therefore, continue to treat the patient with a~figure-of-8 splint and a sling.  She is requesting some stronger analgesics~as she was just placed on Darvocet, and this seems reasonable, so I did~prescribe some Vicodin for her.  Arrangements were made for a follow-up~appointment with Dr. Smith in the orthopedics clinic in approximately nine~days.  The patient works as an iron worker and certainly will not be able~to work at least immediately with her fractured clavicle, so she was~provided with a work excuse until she can follow up with Dr. Smith and he~can determine at which point she may be able to get back to work.

She was referred down to see Dr. Smith today~because the physician who initially evaluated her felt that she would~likely require surgery for her clavicle fracture.  The patient does bring~along her films and in reviewing them it is very doubtful the patient will~require surgery.  I did share the films with Dr. Smith and he is in~agreement that at least at this point the patient will not require any type~of open procedure.  Will, therefore, continue to treat the patient with a~figure-of-8 splint and a sling.  She is requesting some stronger analgesics~as she was just placed on Darvocet, and this seems reasonable, so I did~prescribe some Vicodin for her.  Arrangements were made for a follow-up~appointment with Dr. Smith in the orthopedics clinic in approximately nine~days.  The patient works as an iron worker and certainly will not be able~to work at least immediately with her fractured clavicle, so she was~provided with a work excuse until she can follow up with Dr. Smith and he~can determine at which point she may be able to get back to work.

OBX|1|TX|||Test~~Emergency Room~~The patient is a 39-year-old female who fell off a horse yesterday and~fractured her left clavicle.  She was referred down to see Dr. Smith today~because the physician who initially evaluated her felt that she would~likely require surgery for her clavicle fracture.  The patient does bring~along her films and in reviewing them it is very doubtful the patient will~require surgery.  I did share the films with Dr. Smith and he is in~agreement that at least at this point the patient will not require any type~of open procedure.  Will, therefore, continue to treat the patient with a~figure-of-8 splint and a sling.  She is requesting some stronger analgesics~as she was just placed on Darvocet, and this seems reasonable, so I did~prescribe some Vicodin for her.  Arrangements were made for a follow-up~appointment with Dr. Smith in the orthopedics clinic in approximately nine~days.  The patient works as an iron worker and certainly will not be able~to work at least immediately with her fractured clavicle, so she was~provided with a work excuse until she can follow up with Dr. Smith and he~can determine at which point she may be able to get back to work.
